# {IPEPhyPortMUXCtl}
# -- Close all ports MUX/DEMUX function
# -- 4'b0000: Regular port (No MUX)
# -- 4'b0001: Old VLAN encoded multiplexing
# -- 4'b0010: EVB
# -- 4'b0011: CB downlink
# -- 4'b0100: PE downlink with cascade port
# -- 4'b0101: PE uplink
# -- 4'b0110: BridgeHeader without tunnel
# -- 4'b0111: BridgeHeader with L2
# -- 4'b1000: BridgeHeader with L2 + IPv4
# -- 4'b1001: BridgeHeader with L2 + IPv6
# -- 4'b1010: BridgeHeader IPv4
# -- 4'b1011: BridgeHeader =IPv6
# -- 4'b1100 ~ 4'b1101: Reserved
set-field 0 IpePhyPortMuxCtl 0 muxType 0

# -- The event_port_address field shall have the value 0x013F corresponding to the decimal value 319
# -- The general_port_address field shall have the value 0x0140 corresponding to the decimal value 320

# 2 -- l4Header[15][2:1]
# 3 -- l4Header[15][1:0]

# -- system mac enable
# -- when route port receives bcast arp packet, discard!!

#--  DsMetEntry.portCheckDiscard is valid

set-field 0 MetFifoCtl 0 discardMetLoop 1
# QMgrEnqCtl
#-- if set, srcQueueSelect is masked off if the packet is from fabric
#-- headerHash bits number in BridgeHeader
#-- 3'b1: 3
#-- 3'b2: 4
#-- 3'b3: 5
#-- 3'b4: 6
#-- 3'b5: 7
#-- Other: 8
#-- If set, link aggregation hash computed based on headerHash, else equal to headerHash
#-- Number of bits for queueSelType to be derived from destMap
#-- 2'b00: {3'b000, destMap[15:14]}
#-- 2'b01: {2'b00, destMap[15:13]}
#-- 2'b10: {1'b0, destMap[15:12]}
#-- 2'b11: {destMap[15:11]}
# DsQWriteDestPortChannelMap
# NetworkPort 0~512
# MiscPort 512~640
set-field 0 QWriteSgmacCtl 0 sgmacEn 0

#do not delete after complete DMA 
set-field 0 dsbufretrvexcp 0x013e packetoffsetreset 0

set-field 0 BufferRetrieveCtl 0 exceptionPktEditMode 1

set-field 0 MetFifoCtl 0 portCheckEn 1
#--  Discard packet from fabric and to fabric again
set-field 0 MetFifoCtl 0 discardMetLoop 1
# QMgrEnqCtl
#-- if set, srcQueueSelect is masked off if the packet is from fabric
#-- headerHash bits number in BridgeHeader
#-- 3'b1: 3
#-- 3'b2: 4
#-- 3'b3: 5
#-- 3'b4: 6
#-- 3'b5: 7
#-- Other: 8
#-- If set, link aggregation hash computed based on headerHash, else equal to headerHash
#-- Number of bits for queueSelType to be derived from destMap
#-- 2'b00: {3'b000, destMap[15:14]}
#-- 2'b01: {2'b00, destMap[15:13]}
#-- 2'b10: {1'b0, destMap[15:12]}
#-- 2'b11: {destMap[15:11]}
set-field 0 QWriteSgmacCtl 0 sgmacEn 0
